 The festival of Bhaiya Dooj is celebrated on the second day of Deepawali on Kartik Shukla Dwitiya
 is tithi se yamraj or dwitiya tithi kaa sambandh hone ke kaaran isko yamadvitiya bhi kaha jaataa he

 ’ Milk prices will increase in Delhi and the Capital Region from Wednesday
 shahar or aasapaas ke kshetron main doodh kii aapurti karne vaali company amul ne doodh ke daam main do rupee prati litre badhotaree karne kaa nirnay kiya he
 RS Sodhi, managing director of the Gujarat Cooperative Milk Marketing Association (GCMMF), which sells the Amul brand of milk, said, "we have decided to increase the price of milk by two rupees per liter in Delhi and NCR region
" sodhi ne bataaya ki ab phul kriim doodh kii keemat 40 rupee se badhaakar 42 rupee litak jabaki toned doodh kii keemat 30 rupee se badhaakar 32 rupee prati litre ho jaaegi
 Similarly, the price of double toned milk will be increased from Rs 26 to Rs 28 per liter
 sodhi ne bataaya, kisaanon se hamaare doodh kii kharid laagat badhane or parivahan laagat main badhotaree hone ke kaaran hamane doodh ke daam badhaane kaa nirnay kiya he
 It is noteworthy that Amul is the main milk supplier in the capital and sells around 23 lakh liters of milk daily
 isi prakaar madar deyari kii packaged evam khule (token vaale) doodh kii rojna bikri kareeb 30 lakh litre he

 In such a situation, a call was made to Chief Minister Yogi's Chief Secretary Rajiv Kumar and his subordinate staff at all DM offices at 9 am on Monday 17 July to investigate these district magistrates
